============================================================
-04- COMMANDS
------------------------------------------------------------

?-Earth
-------
??? times, use a random earth-elemental skill.

  (4/8 chance each)  Magnitude8
  (1/8 chance each)  LifeShaver, Quake, Slide, Terrato

?-Shell
-------
??? times, use the skill 'Shell'

BioBlas
-------
Use the skill 'Bio Blaster'

Bolt3
-------
Use the skill 'Bolt 3'

CurLife
-------
Use the combo Cure + LifeShaver.

ImpConf
-------
Use the combo Imp + Confusion.

R-Black
-------
Use a random black magic spell.

  (3/32 chance each)  Doom, Flare
  (2/32 chance each)  Bolt 2, Break, Demi, Poison
  (1/32 chance each)  Bio, Bolt, Bolt 3, Drain, Fire, Fire 2, Fire 3, Ice, Ice 2, Ice 3, Merton, Meteor, Pearl, Quake, Quartr, Ultima, W Wind, X-Zone

R-Chaos
-------
Use a random skill (including broken and glitchy skills).

R-Heal
-------
Use a random HP- and/or MP-restoring skill.
Equal chance of any of the following:
  Cure, Cure 2, Cure 3, Heal Force, Ice Rabbit, Life, Life 2, Mantra, Pearl Wind, Phoenix, Spiraler, Sraphim, Starlet, Sun Bath, Tapir, Wild Bear

R-Ice
-------
Use a random ice-elemental skill.

  (4/16 chance each)  Shiva
  (3/16 chance each)  Ice
  (2/16 chance each)  Absolute 0, Ice 3
  (1/16 chance each)  Blizzard, Ice 2, Ice Beam, Storm, Surge

R-Phys
-------
Use a random physical skill.

  (2/8 chance each)  Dispatch
  (1/8 chance each)  Pummel, Quadra Slam, Quadra Slice, Slash, Suplex, Tentacle

ShiXZon
-------
Use the combo Shimsham + X-Zone.

Slow
-------
Use the skill 'Slow'

XFerImp
-------
Use the combo X-Fer + Imp.
